// CIDM-4382 Notes
    - October 9, 2019

Make sure you have an account for MongoDB: https://www.mongodb.com/
    1.) Create Database and a Cluster
    2. A cluster houses your collections and Database
    Shard is what mongoDB calls its RAID technology. basically distributing pieces of the data to optimize it or create redundancy

Remember VATSIM: http://us.data.vatsim.net/vatsim-data.txt
- Text files tell you how to read them at the top

Our first task will be to see if we can read from a database file
PARTSVATSIM IS NOT DONE! Dr. Babb is just pointing us in the right direction for the application
All this data is ONE string, the breaks are just specified to be "/n".

Transmissitable data is not clean or usuable data

!<COLLECTIONNAME>: starts a new table for data


Babb wants us to prove to him that we can extract data from this database and send it to the screen.

What Babb does is send it to the screen on a table.

        console.log("DUDE " + new Date().toTimeString());    

The next few days are focused on the question "Can you read from a database"
If you want to send something to the browser use a .pug template
IF you want to send something to the console use console.Log

Retrieval of data is from 

    let task = cron.schedule('*/2 * * * *', () => {

   axios.get('http://us.data.vatsim.net/vatsim-data.txt')
    .then( (response) => {
        parseVATSIM(response.data);
    })
    .catch( (error) => {
        console.log(error);
    });

});

                class Client {

                    /*
                    callsign:cid:realname:clienttype:frequency:latitude:longitude:altitude:groundspeed:groundspeed:planned_tascruise:planned_depairport:planned_altitude:planned_destairport:server:protrevision:rating:transponder:facilitytype:visualrange:planned_revision:planned_flighttype:planned_deptime:planned_actdeptime:planned_hrsenroute:planned_minenroute:planned_hrsfuel:planned_minfuel:planned_altairport:planned_remarks:planned_route:planned_depairport_lat:planned_depairport_lon:planned_destairport_lat:planned_destairport_lon:atis_message:time_last_atis_received:time_logon:heading:QNH_iHg:QNH_Mb:

                const parseVATSIM = (data) => {

                    let start = false;

                    lines = data.split("\n");

                    lines.forEach(element => {

                        parts = element.split(':');
                        
                        // callsign:
                        let callsign = parts[0];

                        if(callsign.startsWith("!SERVERS")){
                            start = false;
                        } 
                        
                        if(!callsign.startsWith(";") && !callsign.startsWith(" ") && start){
                            console.log(`Callsign: ${callsign}`);
                        } 

                        if(callsign.startsWith("!CLIENTS")){
                            start = true;
                        }         
                        
                        // cid:
                        // realname:
                        // clienttype:
                        // frequency:
                        // latitude:
                        // longitude:
                        // altitude:
                        // groundspeed:
                        // planned_aircraft:
                        // planned_tascruise:
                        // planned_depairport:
                        // planned_altitude:
                        // planned_destairport:
                        // server:
                        // protrevision:
                        // rating:
                        // transponder:
                        // facilitytype:
                        // visualrange:
                        // planned_revision:
                        // planned_flighttype:
                        // planned_deptime:

                        // heading:

                        // QNH_Mb:

                    });

                    console.log("DUDE " + new Date().toTimeString());    

                };

                let task = cron.schedule('*/2 * * * *', () => {

                    .then( (response) => {
                        parseVATSIM(response.data);
